### [1] [WaveLander: A Generalizable Hierarchical Control Framework for UAV Landing on Wave-Disturbed Platforms via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01281)
*Chun-Kit Li,Iok Long Sit,Ming Fung Siu,Ka Yu Kui,Hin Wang Lin,Pengyu Wang,Ling Shi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: WaveLander 提出一种分层强化学习框架，将无人机在晃动海面平台上的自主降落解耦为高层垂直降落决策与低层飞行稳定控制，以紧凑的相对观测映射标量垂直速度参考，实现无需显式切换规则的平滑着陆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于模型的方法依赖精确运动预测和在线优化，端到端学习方法训练复杂度高、可解释性差，而无人机在波浪扰动平台上的降落面临随机运动、时变姿态和不确定触地条件的挑战，因此需要一种兼顾鲁棒性与简洁性的新方法。

Method: 提出 WaveLander 分层控制框架：高层采用强化学习策略，将紧凑的平台相对观测映射为标量垂直速度参考，实现时序感知的降落决策；低层采用传统飞控维持姿态稳定和横向跟踪。该设计将动态平台降落问题降维为低维时序控制问题，无需显式切换规则即可产生平滑着陆行为。

Result: 在随机波浪诱导平台运动的仿真实验中，WaveLander 实现了鲁棒的着陆性能，并能泛化至未见过的扰动条件。

Conclusion: 分层学习控制方法在海上无人机回收场景中具有潜力，为动态平台自主降落提供了有效且可解释的解决方案。

Abstract: Autonomous landing of unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) on wave-disturbed marine platforms remains challenging due to stochastic platform motion, time-varying platform attitude, and uncertain touchdown conditions. Existing model-based methods often require accurate motion prediction and online optimization, while end-to-end learning approaches may suffer from high training complexity and limited interpretability. This paper presents WaveLander, a hierarchical control framework via reinforcement learning (RL) that decouples vertical landing decision-making from low-level flight stabilization. The RL policy maps a compact platform-relative observation to a scalar vertical velocity reference, while a conventional low-level flight controller maintains attitude stability and lateral tracking. This formulation reduces dynamic platform landing to a low-dimensional, timing-aware control problem and enables smooth landing behavior without explicit switching rules. Simulation results under randomized wave-induced platform motions show that WaveLander achieves robust landing performance and generalizes to unseen disturbance conditions, demonstrating the potential of hierarchical learning-based control for marine UAV recovery.

</details>


### [2] [Adaptive Companionship for Group-Following Robots: Handling Dynamically Changing Group Formations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01287)
*Cong-Thanh Vu,Yen-Chen Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于视觉语言模型（VLM）的自适应群体陪伴方法，使社交机器人能够推理陪伴位置、保持社交距离并理解群体动态，结合MPPI控制器保证安全稳定，实验表明成功率提升15%、碰撞率降低25%，且用户感知行为自然得体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类群体通常不遵循固定队形，这对机器人维持自然陪伴行为构成重大挑战。现有方法难以灵活应对群体动态变化，需要一种能理解社交语义的解决方案。

Method: 首先检测群体成员，通过感知模块生成交互群体空间的视觉表征作为VLM输入，利用VLM的语义推理能力推断陪伴位置、社交距离和群体动态；然后将VLM的推理结果与模型预测路径积分（MPPI）控制器结合，确保运动的稳定性与安全性。

Result: 在五个场景的实验评估中，所提方法相比基线方法成功率提升15%，碰撞率降低25%；用户研究表明生成的陪伴行为被认为自然且符合社交规范。

Conclusion: 该方法有效解决了机器人在非固定队形群体中的自然陪伴问题，验证了VLM语义推理与MPPI控制结合的可行性和优越性，为人机社交交互提供了新思路。

Abstract: Accompanying a group of humans is an essential aspect of developing human-like social cognition in robots. However, human groups typically do not follow fixed formations, which poses significant challenges for robots in maintaining natural companionship behaviors. In this paper, we propose an adaptive group-accompaniment method for social robots based on Vision-Language Models (VLMs), leveraging their semantic reasoning capabilities to infer companion positions, maintain social distances, and understand group dynamics. The members of the group are first detected, and a perceptual module generates visual representations of the interaction group space as input to the VLM, which is then combined with a Model Predictive Path Integral (MPPI) controller to ensure stability and safety. Experimental evaluations across five scenarios show that the proposed method enables robots to accompany the group effectively, demonstrating a 15\% improvement in success rate and a 25\% reduction in collision rate compared to baseline approaches. Additionally, a user study indicates that the generated companionship behaviors are perceived as natural and socially appropriate.

</details>


### [3] [The Three Dimensions of ROS 2 Middleware](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01304)
*Sanghoon Lee,Taehun Kim,Angelo Corsaro,Kyung-Joon Park*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了ROS 2中间件（DDS、Zenoh等）在动态无线环境下的架构局限性，提出Space（空间）、Time（时间）、State（状态）三个结构维度作为分析框架，揭示了这三者之间的结构性权衡，并规划了未来机器人中间件的研究路线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ROS 2虽已成为机器人软件开发的事实标准，但其底层中间件（DDS、Zenoh等）在动态、资源受限的无线环境中存在结构性局限。现有研究缺乏一个统一的概念框架来系统分析这些局限，导致对空间抽象、时间可预测性和状态连续性之间深层权衡的理解不足。

Method: 提出三维概念框架——Space（从物理拓扑到模块化部署的空间抽象）、Time（控制回路的时序可预测性）、State（动态节点参与和间歇连接下的上下文连续性）。在此框架下，对ROS 2中间件架构、发现机制、数据交换和状态管理机制进行结构化分析，并通过综合现有文献，梳理三者间的结构性权衡关系。

Result: 在受限无线条件下，空间抽象会掩盖网络可变性并削弱时序保障；维持状态连续性的机制引入计算与网络开销，与时间关键通信形成竞争。这三个维度之间存在不可消除的结构性权衡，构成了当代机器人中间件的实际性能边界。

Conclusion: 当前中间件在Space-Time-State三个维度上的权衡揭示了其架构极限。文章指出现有建模与分析方法存在空白，并据此提出了一条面向鲁棒、可扩展机器人中间件架构的原则性研究路线图。

Abstract: ROS 2 (Robot Operating System 2) has emerged as the de facto standard for modern robot software development, with middleware implementations such as the Data Distribution Service (DDS) and Zenoh forming the core infrastructure for distributed robotic communication. Despite their architectural flexibility, these middleware systems exhibit structural limitations, particularly under dynamic and resource-constrained wireless environments. This paper presents a systematic survey of ROS 2 middleware and introduces a conceptual framework to examine its architectural limits through three structural dimensions required by distributed robotic systems, namely Space, Time, and State. We first provide a structured analysis of middleware architecture and operational dynamics, including discovery, data exchange, and state management mechanisms. Building on this foundation, we formalize Time as temporal predictability for control loops, Space as spatial abstraction from physical topology to enable modular deployment, and State as contextual continuity despite dynamic node participation and intermittent connectivity. Through a comprehensive review of existing implementations and prior studies, we organize middleware research according to the structural trade-offs that arise among these dimensions. Under constrained wireless conditions, spatial abstraction can obscure network variability and weaken temporal guarantees, while mechanisms that preserve state continuity introduce computational and network overhead that competes with time-critical communication. These interactions reveal structural trade-offs that characterize the practical limits of contemporary robot middleware. By synthesizing architectural patterns and identifying gaps in current modeling and analysis approaches, this survey outlines a principled research roadmap for robust and scalable robotic middleware architectures.

</details>


### [4] [Neuro-Symbolic Safety Guidance for Vision-Language-Action Models via Constrained Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01378)
*William English,Hao Zheng,Rickard Ewetz*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种面向基于流匹配的VLA模型的神经符号安全引导机制，通过在去噪过程中对中间轨迹预测施加最小范数约束优化，实现预测性碰撞避免，在SafeLIBERO基准上显著优于单步安全方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型的安全措施仅能防止机器人下一步动作引发的碰撞，缺乏预见性。面对长时域任务中累积分布偏移加剧的问题，亟需一种能够提前预判并规避碰撞的预测性安全机制。

Method: 将安全约束执行建模为最小范数约束优化问题，在流匹配的迭代去噪过程中，对每一步产生的含噪中间轨迹预测进行分析与修正。通过将符号化约束满足与神经轨迹生成交替执行，实现对尚未发生但可预见的碰撞进行提前纠正。

Result: 在SafeLIBERO基准上，该方法实现82.8%的碰撞避免率和81.6%的任务成功率，相较单步方法分别提升6.3%和19.8%，在长时域任务上提升尤为显著。

Conclusion: 将符号约束优化嵌入神经轨迹生成的去噪过程，实现了从被动响应到预测性避碰的范式转变，为VLA模型的安全部署提供了有效路径。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have demonstrated promising generalization capabilities across robotic manipulation tasks, yet their real-world deployment remains limited by the lack of effective safety measures. Specifically, existing safety measures only prevent collisions caused by the robot's next action. In this paper, we propose a neuro-symbolic safety guidance mechanism for flow matching based VLAs that enables predictive collision avoidance. Flow matching based VLAs determine the next actions by predicting a trajectory (a sequence of actions) through an iterative neural flow matching process. Our method formulates safety enforcement as a minimum-norm constrained optimization problem that corrects safety violations during the denoising process of noisy intermediate trajectory predictions. By analyzing predicted trajectories and applying corrections during iterative denoising, our approach anticipates collisions before they become unavoidable. This interleaving of symbolic constraint satisfaction with neural trajectory generation enables predictive collision avoidance rather than reactive intervention. On the SafeLIBERO benchmark, our method achieves 82.8% collision avoidance and 81.6% task success, a 6.3% and 19.8% improvement respectively over single-step methods, with the largest gains on long-horizon tasks where compounding distribution shift is most pronounced. Video demonstrations of our approach are included on our project page at https://willenglish.tech/SafetyGuidedFlowMatching/.

</details>


### [5] [CommonRoad-Game: A Human-in-the-Loop Simulation Framework for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01382)
*Yunfei Bi,Youran Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: CommonRoad-Game 是一个轻量化的人机交互仿真框架，与 CommonRoad 平台深度集成，旨在通过多线程架构和时钟同步机制，实现对运动规划器的系统化人机交互测试与人类驾驶行为分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有仿真平台存在三大缺陷：(1) 依赖离线录制数据集，缺乏实时人机交互接口；(2) 与自动驾驶生态系统集成度不足；(3) 计算开销大，不适用于早期自动驾驶研究中快速原型开发和灵活实验。因此需要一个轻量、实时、可交互的仿真框架来系统评估运动规划算法在人类参与场景下的安全性和效率。

Method: 提出了 CommonRoad-Game 框架，核心设计包括：(1) 多线程架构与鲁棒同步机制，将仿真时间与挂钟时间对齐，确保自动驾驶车辆与人类驾驶车辆之间具有确定性且时间一致的交互；(2) 场景生成模块，通过记录驾驶日志，从人机交互实验中构建多样化且可复现的测试用例；(3) 无缝集成 CommonRoad 兼容的运动规划器，生成交互式驾驶场景。

Result: 实验结果表明，CommonRoad-Game 实现了稳定的时间同步，支持可扩展的多智能体仿真，并能无缝集成 CommonRoad 兼容的运动规划器以生成交互式驾驶场景。

Conclusion: CommonRoad-Game 有效填补了现有仿真平台在轻量化、实时人机交互和生态集成方面的空白，为自动驾驶运动规划的早期研究提供了高效、灵活的测试工具。

Abstract: Motion planning algorithms should be evaluated in human-in-the-loop environments to ensure they produce safe and efficient behaviors during interactions. However, existing simulation platforms often rely on recorded datasets, lack dedicated interfaces for real-time human interaction, or remain weakly integrated with an autonomous driving ecosystem. Moreover, many human-in-the-loop simulators are computationally intensive by design, making them less suitable for rapid prototyping and flexible experimentation in early-stage autonomous driving research. To address these limitations, we present CommonRoad-Game, a lightweight human-in-the-loop simulation framework tightly integrated with the CommonRoad platform, focusing on the systematic testing of motion planners with human participation and the analysis of human driving behaviors in interactive scenarios. We introduce a multi-threaded architecture with a robust synchronization mechanism that aligns simulation time with wall-clock time, enabling deterministic and temporally consistent interaction between autonomous and human-driven vehicles. In addition, the framework provides a scenario generation module that records driving logs, allowing diverse and reproducible test cases to be constructed from human-in-the-loop experiments. Experimental results demonstrate that CommonRoad-Game achieves stable temporal synchronization, supports scalable multi-agent simulation, and seamlessly integrates CommonRoad-compatible motion planners to generate interactive driving scenarios. The source code is publicly available at https://github.com/Yunfei-Bi8/CommonRoad-Game.

</details>


### [6] [BIFROST: Bridging Invariant Feature Representation for Observation-space Sim2Real Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01410)
*Yunfu Deng,Josiah P. Hanna*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: BIFROST 利用跨域互模拟目标，在配对跨域数据上学习共享历史编码器，将导致等效长期行为的观察-动作序列映射到相近的潜在状态，从而使在仿真中训练的策略能够零样本迁移到现实环境，有效应对视觉与动力学双重域差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 sim2real 迁移方法通常通过分离的适配模块分别处理视觉差距和动力学差距，然后将两者组合或叠加。然而，sim2real 的根本前提是仿真与现实任务之间存在共享结构——等效的配置下等效的动作应产生等效的长期结果。本文旨在从原始观察中识别并利用这一共享结构，实现零样本迁移。

Method: 提出 BIFROST 方法，核心是在配对跨域数据上学习一个共享历史编码器，采用跨域互模拟（cross-domain bisimulation）目标：无论来自仿真域还是现实域，只要观察-动作序列导致等效的长期行为，就被映射到相邻的潜在状态。在此潜在状态空间上训练的策略可直接零样本迁移到现实环境。

Result: 在 sim2sim 视觉导航任务以及 sim2real 接触丰富操作任务和视觉伺服任务上进行了实验验证。结果表明，BIFROST 在同时存在视觉域差距和动力学域差距的场景下能够实现有效迁移，而域适应和联合训练基线方法均失败。

Conclusion: BIFROST 通过跨域互模拟学习共享表征，成功捕捉了仿真与现实之间的任务共享结构，实现了从仿真到现实的零样本策略迁移，在视觉和动力学双重域差距下显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Sim2real transfer for robot policy learning suffers due to mismatch between simulation and reality. Existing methods typically address each gap in isolation through separate adaptation modules, which are composed or layered when both gaps coexist. Yet the basis for attempting sim2real in the first place is that there is shared structure between a task in simulation and reality, where equivalent actions from equivalent configurations produce equivalent long term outcomes regardless of domain specific differences in rendering or physics. In this paper, we study whether we can identify and exploit this shared structure from raw observations to train a policy that enables zero shot transfer. We introduce BIFROST, which learns a shared history encoder on paired cross-domain data via cross-domain bisimulation objective: observation-action sequences leading to equivalent long-term behavior are mapped to nearby latent states, regardless of domain. Policies trained on these latent states in simulation transfer zero-shot to reality. We provide empirical evidence on sim2sim visual navigation and sim2real contact rich manipulation task and visual servoing task that BIFROST achieves effective transfer where domain adaptation and co-training baselines fail under both visual and dynamics domain gaps.

</details>


### [7] [SE(2) Navigation Mesh](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01454)
*Shuyang Shi,Kaixian Qu,Changan Chen,Ines Kast,Yuntao Ma,Marco Hutter*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出SE(2)导航网格，将偏航角相关可通行性编码到多边形导航网格中，结合ASA路径规划策略和在线增量更新方法，显著提升非圆形机器人在受限环境中的导航能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有导航网格假设偏航角无关可通行性，对非圆形机器人在狭窄空间（如门口、走廊拐角）的导航不适用；点云和体素占用地图缺乏显式表面结构，而直接在稠密三角网格上做路径规划计算代价过高。

Method: 提出SE(2) NavMesh：用足迹掩码评估偏航依赖可通行性，构建偏航分层图并编码平移与旋转连接关系；开发ASA（A*-String Pulling-A*）分层路径规划策略，先优化位置再优化朝向；提出从流式点云在线增量更新SE(2) NavMesh的方法，与几何重建并发执行。

Result: 仿真中SE(2) NavMesh比经典NavMesh多捕获50%以上可通行区域；ASA管道在受限环境中持续优于基于采样的基线方法；真实机器人实验验证了多环境下的实时在线生成与成功导航。

Conclusion: SE(2) NavMesh为复杂多层环境中非圆形地面机器人提供了一种高效、准确的偏航依赖可通行性表征，结合ASA规划和在线更新能力，在理论和实践上均展现出优越性。

Abstract: Global navigation for ground robots in complex multi-level environments requires representations that accurately capture traversable regions while enabling efficient path planning. Current approaches present key limitations: Point clouds and volumetric occupancy maps lack explicit surface structure for traversability estimation, whereas direct pathfinding on dense triangle meshes is computationally prohibitive. Navigation meshes mitigate these challenges through polygonal abstraction of the underlying mesh, but assume yaw-invariant traversability, rendering them unsuitable for non-circular robots in constrained spaces. We propose SE(2) Navigation Mesh (SE(2) NavMesh), a polygonal representation of traversable regions that encodes yaw-dependent traversability. Our method evaluates traversability using footprint masks and constructs a graph over yaw-specific layers with explicit translational and rotational connectivity. Grounded in this representation, we develop an A*-String Pulling-A* (ASA) pathfinding strategy that hierarchically optimizes robot position and heading. We also present an online method that incrementally updates the SE(2) NavMesh from streaming point clouds during concurrent geometry reconstruction. In simulation, the SE(2) NavMesh captures over 50% more traversable area than classical NavMeshes, and the SE(2) NavMesh + ASA pipeline consistently outperforms sampling-based baselines in constrained environments. Extensive real-world experiments on a physical robot validate real-time online generation and successful navigation across multiple environments.

</details>


### [8] [A Reconfigurable Rocker-Bogie Robot for High Step Climbing and Turning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01554)
*Kento Koizumi,Tomoaki Ohba,Yuta Saito,Takeya Morito,Kenji Suzuki*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种可重构摇臂-转向架机构，通过主动摆动的转向架关节实现四轮/六轮构型切换，结合全向轮实现高效零半径转弯，转弯速度是传统构型的5倍以上，同时保持40 cm的越障能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统摇臂-转向架（rocker-bogie）机构虽然越障能力强，但六轮非转向抓地轮导致转弯效率低下、转弯半径大、轮子扭矩消耗高。如何在保持高越障性能的前提下，用少量驱动器实现高效转弯，是亟待解决的问题。

Method: 1）在转向架关节（bogie joints）安装电机，主动控制转向架上下摆动，实现在四轮构型与六轮构型之间切换；2）在摇臂后端安装全向轮（omnidirectional wheels），使四轮构型下基于差速驱动模型实现平滑转弯；3）搭建原型机器人进行实验验证，对比传统六轮非转向抓地轮构型的转弯速度与轮扭矩，并测试越障能力。

Result: 1）零半径转弯速度达到传统摇臂-转向架机构（六轮非转向抓地轮）的5倍以上；2）总平均轮扭矩仅为传统构型的约17%；3）成功攀爬40 cm台阶，平均攀爬时间6.4秒。

Conclusion: 所提出的可重构摇臂-转向架机构在显著提升转弯效率、大幅降低轮扭矩的同时，保持了出色的越障性能，验证了该设计方案在移动机器人领域的有效性和优越性。

Abstract: This study proposes a reconfigurable rocker-bogie mechanism that achieves efficient turning motion with a small number of actuators while maintaining high step-climbing capability. By installing motors at the bogie joints and actively swinging up and down bogies, the system enables switching between four-wheel and six-wheel configurations. Omnidirectional wheels are mounted on the rear ends of the rockers, allowing smooth turning in the four-wheel configuration based on a differential-drive model. Experimental evaluation using a prototype robot demonstrated that the proposed mechanism achieves zero-radius turning at a speed more than five times that of a conventional rocker-bogie mechanism equipped with six non-steerable grip wheels, while requiring only approximately 17% of the total average wheel torque. In addition, the robot successfully climbed a 40 cm step with an average climbing time of 6.4 s, confirming its high turning and step-climbing performance.

</details>


### [9] [Multi-Rate Nonlinear Model Predictive Control for Wall-Supported Bipedal Locomotion of Quadrupedal Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01574)
*Taizoon Chunawala,Jeeseop Kim,Kaveh Akbari Hamed*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种基于多速率非线性模型预测控制（MR-NMPC）的分层规划与控制框架，使四足机器人在受限环境中实现靠墙辅助的双足混合运动，在高速不规则地形上成功率较传统方法提升2.9倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四足机器人在受限环境中执行靠墙辅助双足运动时，需要同时规划接触点序列和质心/姿态连续轨迹，并处理单边接触约束、欠驱动和动力学切换等难题。传统启发式落足策略缺乏动态稳定性保障，因此需要一种能统一优化接触点与质心轨迹的实时控制方法。

Method: 提出分层框架：(1) 上层采用MR-NMPC，基于单刚体（SRB）动力学模型，在多速率最优控制框架内同时规划接触点离散时间轨迹和质心/姿态连续时间轨迹；(2) 下层采用基于虚拟约束和二次规划的非线性全身控制器（WBC），强制执行全阶动力学并跟踪上层参考轨迹。

Result: 在Unitree A1四足机器人上进行了大量数值仿真验证，展示了在粗糙地形和外部扰动下受限环境中的鲁棒靠墙双足运动。对比分析表明，在高速通过不规则地形时，所提MR-NMPC比传统基于启发式落足的MPC成功率高出2.9倍。

Conclusion: MR-NMPC通过将接触点规划纳入多速率最优控制框架，显著提升了动态稳定性和地形适应能力，相比传统启发式策略具有明显优势，为四足机器人在受限环境中的混合运动提供了有效的实时控制方案。

Abstract: This paper presents a novel layered planning and control framework based on multi-rate nonlinear model predictive control (MR-NMPC) that enables quadrupedal robots to perform hybrid bipedal locomotion with wall-assisted support in constrained environments. Real-time trajectory optimization for this locomotion presents significant challenges, as the controller must simultaneously plan for both the contact points and the continuous trajectories of the robot's center of mass (CoM) and orientation within the robot's nonlinear dynamics while accounting for unilateral contact constraints, underactuation, and the switching nature of the robot's dynamics. At the high level of the control framework, an MR-NMPC is proposed, which dynamically plans both the discrete-time trajectories of the contact points and the continuous-time trajectories of the CoM and orientation, using a single rigid body (SRB) dynamics model. By incorporating contact-point planning within the multi-rate optimal control framework, this approach enhances dynamic stability compared to heuristic foot placement strategies. At the low level of the control framework, a nonlinear whole-body controller (WBC) based on virtual constraints and a quadratic program enforces full-order dynamics and tracks the MR-NMPC references. The proposed approach is validated through extensive numerical simulations demonstrating the robust wall-assisted bipedal locomotion of a Unitree A1 quadrupedal robot on rough terrains and under external disturbances in a constrained environment. Comparative analysis shows that the proposed MR-NMPC achieves a 2.9 times higher success rate compared to conventional MPC with heuristic-based foot placement strategies in negotiating irregular terrain at high speeds.

### [10] [Path planning for unmanned naval surface vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01631)
*Daniel G. Schwartz*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向无人水面艇(USV)的双层路径规划框架：全局规划器创新性地结合了Grassfire、改进的Grassfire和新版概率路图(PRM)三种算法；局部规划器则通过高层决策逻辑，根据障碍物相对于全局路径的运动方向，智能地选择从障碍物后方绕行的策略，而非平行跟随等待超车机会。仿真验证了方法的有效性，并与D*等算法进行了对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: USV在固定障碍物与移动障碍物（船只、游泳者、其他USV等）的实时避障方面仍面临诸多挑战。现有动态路径规划系统（如D*）通常不会将USV引导至移动障碍物后方绕行，缺乏系统的避障决策逻辑。因此，需要一种能够智能决策绕行策略的全局-局部协同规划方法。

Method: 方法分为两层：(1)全局路径规划器——组合使用三种算法：经典的Grassfire算法、一种对Grassfire的改进变体，以及一种更直观的新版概率路图(PRM)，用于在已知固定障碍物环境中规划从起点到终点的路径；(2)局部路径规划器——采用高层决策逻辑，通过观察移动障碍物相对于USV全局路径的运动方向，系统性地引导USV从障碍物后方绕行，避免平行跟随直至出现超车机会的被动策略。

Result: 通过仿真验证了所提方法的有效性。仿真中实现了经典的D*算法作为对比基准，讨论部分进一步涵盖了其他动态路径规划系统，这些系统与D*一样，未必能主动将USV路由至移动障碍物后方进行规避。

Conclusion: 所提出的全局-局部双层规划方法能够有效处理USV的固定和移动障碍物避障问题，特别是局部规划器的高层决策逻辑实现了更优的绕行策略——主动从移动障碍物后方通过，优于传统方法中平行跟随的策略。该方法在仿真中得到了验证。

Abstract: There nowadays is a myriad of approaches to real-time avoidance of fixed obstacles for unmanned surface vehicles (USVs) and, to a lesser extent, also the task of avoiding moving obstacles such as boats, ships, swimmers, and other USVs, but both topics still present challenges. This paper offers novel approaches to both of these problems. It uses a combination of a global path planner, which finds a path from a start point to a goal point that avoids fixed obstacles (given that their locations are known in advance), and a local path planner, which can circumnavigate a moving obstacle (as well as any previously unknown fixed obstacles). The global planner is novel in that it employs a combination of three path planners, one known in the literature as Grassfire, one that is a new modification of Grassfire, and one that is a new, and arguably more intuitive, version of the well-known Probabilistic Roadmap. The local planner is novel in that it employs a higher-level decision logic based on its observations regarding the direction of movement of the obstacle relative to the USVs global path. This logic enables the USV to determine the best strategy for avoiding the obstacle by systematically routing the vehicle behind the obstacle rather than running parallel to it until the opportunity to pass appears. Simulations are provided that validate these claims. For comparison with other systems, the simulations include an implementation of the well-known D* algorithm, and the discussion covers additional dynamic path planning systems, which, like D*, do not necessarily route the vehicle behind the moving obstacle.

### [11] [One Demonstration Is Enough for Real-World Robotic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01651)
*Yuwan Liu,Hongze Yu,Song Liu,Yuhan Wang,Junge Zhang,Yaodong Yang,Yuanpei Chen,Ceyao Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: AutoSERL 是一个仅需单次演示即可全自动完成真实机器人强化学习干预的框架，通过滑动窗口干预、安全恢复和干预终止三个机制，在六项接触密集型操作任务上超越多个基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实机器人强化学习面临数据采集成本高和奖励设计困难两大挑战。现有结合演示的方法要么需要大量演示，要么依赖训练过程中持续的人工干预。本文旨在仅用单次演示实现干预过程的完全自动化。

Method: 提出 AutoSERL 框架，包含三个互补机制：(1) 滑动窗口干预机制，持续引导探索以防止局部最优和不安全偏离；(2) 安全恢复机制，通过预定义轨迹恢复点检测并纠正失败状态；(3) 干预终止准则，在策略能独立完成任务后自动禁用引导，保留其自主探索优势。

Result: 在两个机器人平台、六项接触密集型操作任务（插入、悬挂、铰链类）上评估，AutoSERL 一致优于使用 20 次演示初始化的 SERL、行为克隆和一 shot 模仿学习基线 MILES，并在插入任务上达到 100% 成功率，同时匹配 HIL-SERL，且对位置变化具有更强鲁棒性。

Conclusion: AutoSERL 证明了仅凭单次演示即可在真实机器人强化学习中实现全自动、安全且高效的策略学习，消除了对持续人工干预的依赖。

Abstract: Learning effective robot control policies on physical hardware is challenging due to costly data collection and the difficulty of reward specification. Prior work has incorporated demonstrations into reinforcement learning (RL), yet existing approaches either require large numbers of demonstrations or depend on continuous human intervention during training. To address these limitations, we present AutoSERL, a framework that leverages a single demonstration to fully automate the intervention process in real-world robot RL. The framework includes three complementary mechanisms to accomplish certain tasks: a sliding window intervention mechanism that continuously guides exploration to prevent local optima and unsafe deviations, a safety recovery mechanism that detects and corrects failure states via predefined trajectory recovery points, and an intervention termination criterion that automatically disables guidance once the policy can independently complete the task, preserving its exploration advantage. We evaluate AutoSERL on six contact-intensive manipulation tasks across two robot platforms, spanning insertion, hanging, and hinge-based tasks. AutoSERL consistently outperforms SERL initialized with 20 demonstrations, behavior cloning, and MILES -- a dedicated one-shot imitation learning baseline -- across all tasks while matching HIL-SERL, achieves 100% success rate on insertion tasks, and demonstrates improved robustness to positional variations, all from a single demonstration. Code and videos are available on our project website: https://autoserl.github.io/.

*Zhiyuan Zhang,Adeesh Desai,Jyun-Chi Hu,Yosuke Saka,Quan Khanh Luu,Jiuzhou Lei,Davood Soleymanzadeh,Bihao Zhang,Minghui Zheng,Yu She*

TL;DR: TacImag 是一个触觉想象框架，在部署时仅用视觉和本体感知预测触觉信号来引导操作策略，无需实际触觉传感器，在真实实验中力场想象提升接触敏感任务44.4%，触觉图像想象提升纹理敏感任务23.3%。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 TacImag 框架：从成对的视触觉演示中训练模型，利用视觉和本体感知预测触觉观测（力场或触觉图像）；在测试时仅凭视觉输入生成想象中的触觉信号，作为额外监督来引导操作策略。

Result: 在6项仿真和4项真实世界操作任务中验证。真实实验中，力场想象使接触敏感任务平均提升44.4%，触觉图像想象使纹理敏感任务平均提升23.3%。研究还表明，触觉想象并非简单恢复缺失的触觉测量，而是将微妙的视觉交互线索转化为策略更易利用的表示。

Conclusion: 触觉想象是可行的，能从视觉中预测触觉信号并提升操作性能；其有效性取决于触觉表示与任务需求的匹配关系；触觉想象本质上是一种接触感知监督，能转化而非单纯复现触觉信号。

Abstract: Tactile sensing can substantially improve contact-rich robotic manipulation, yet its practical deployment remains limited by the fragility, calibration requirements, and maintenance burden of tactile hardware. This raises a fundamental question: can robots benefit from tactile knowledge without requiring tactile sensors at deployment? We present TacImag, a tactile imagination framework that predicts tactile observations from vision and proprioception and uses the generated signals to guide manipulation policies. Trained from paired visuotactile demonstrations, TacImag enables touch-informed manipulation using only visual observations at test time. We evaluate TacImag on six simulated and four real-world manipulation tasks. Across simulation and real-world experiments, imagined tactile observations consistently improve manipulation performance without requiring tactile hardware. In real-world experiments, imagined force fields improve contact-sensitive tasks by 44.4% on average, whereas imagined tactile images improve texture-sensitive tasks by 23.3%, revealing that the effectiveness of tactile imagination depends strongly on the relationship between tactile representation and task requirements. Our results further suggest that tactile imagination does not simply recover missing tactile measurements. Instead, it acts as a form of contact-aware supervision that transforms subtle visual interaction cues into representations that are easier for manipulation policies to exploit.

### [13] [CoRe: Combined Rewards with Vision-Language Model Feedback for Preference-Aligned Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01721)
*Hexian Ni,Tao Lu,Yinghao Cai*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: CoRe提出了一种混合奖励框架，将显式设计的形式化奖励(FR)与从视频偏好中学习的残差奖励(RR)相结合，利用视觉语言模型(VLM)自动构建高效且符合人类偏好的奖励信号，在多个机器人操作任务上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出CoRe框架，包含两个核心模块：(1) 形式化奖励模块(FRM)，利用VLM根据任务知识和偏好反馈迭代设计与优化形式化奖励，使策略在训练中持续改进；(2) 残差奖励模块(RRM)，通过VLM生成视频级别的偏好标签，从中学习残差奖励以捕捉FR未能覆盖的隐式细微偏好。两者协同实现自动化的高效偏好对齐奖励构建。

Result: 在10个仿真机器人操作任务和5个真实世界任务上的大量实验表明，CoRe在策略学习效果和效率上均优于现有方法。

Abstract: Reward design remains a central challenge in reinforcement learning (RL). Hand-crafted rewards are often difficult to specify and may lead to suboptimal policies, while learned rewards from preferences can suffer from inefficiency and unstable training. Inspired by the dual nature of human learning explored in cognitive science, we decompose rewards into two complementary components: Formal Rewards (FR), explicitly designed based on task knowledge, and Residual Rewards (RR), learned from observations to capture implicit and nuanced preferences. Based on this decomposition, we propose CoRe, a hybrid framework that integrates FR and RR with vision-language models (VLMs) feedback to achieve preference-aligned policies without human involvement. Our contributions are twofold: (1) We propose a Formal Reward Module (FRM) that leverages VLMs to iteratively design and optimize FR based on task knowledge and preference feedback, enabling the continual improvement of policy during training; (2) We introduce a Residual Reward Module (RRM) that learns RR from video-level preference by employing VLMs to generate preference labels and capturing nuanced rewards that complement FR, ensuring alignment with human intent. Through the synergy of FRM and RRM, CoRe enables the automatic construction of reliable rewards that are efficient and preference-aligned. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CoRe outperforms existing approaches in terms of policy learning effectiveness and efficiency on ten robotic manipulation tasks in simulation and five real-worlds. Videos can be found on our project website: https://core-2026.github.io/

### [14] [Lightweight Safe Reinforcement Learning for End-to-End UAV Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01794)
*Shenghui Zhang,YuXuan Gao,Songwei Zhao,Jifeng Hu,Zijing Zhang,Hechang Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种面向无人机导航的安全约束感知-控制一体化框架，采用轻量网络编码稀疏观测、分层控制架构下的约束马尔可夫决策过程建模、基于拉格朗日的安全PPO算法及课程学习，实现高速飞行下更高的成功率、安全性与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出安全约束的感知-控制一体化框架：(1) 轻量网络采用非对称卷积与深度可分离卷积，将稀疏观测编码为碰撞风险感知特征；(2) 将导航任务建模为分层控制架构下的约束马尔可夫决策过程(CMDP)；(3) 采用基于拉格朗日的安全PPO算法求解；(4) 引入课程学习提升训练稳定性。

Result: 在不同障碍物密度和飞行速度条件下的实验表明，该方法相比现有RL基线，取得了更高的成功率、更好的安全性和更优的效率。

Abstract: With the rapid development of autonomous aerial systems, Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAVs) are increasingly deployed in applications such as inspection, environmental monitoring, and rescue, creating growing demand for reliable autonomous navigation. However, autonomous UAV navigation in dense environments remains challenging under sparse perception and dynamic constraints. Most reinforcement learning (RL) methods lack explicit safety mechanisms, leading to unsafe exploration, unstable training, and risky behaviors, especially during high-speed flight. Even in safe RL approaches, safety is often enforced by projecting policy outputs onto a safe action set, which may introduce instability. Meanwhile, many learning-based methods rely on dense inputs or large networks, increasing computational burden and limiting lightweight onboard deployment. Facing the above challenges, we propose a safety-constrained perception-control integrated framework for UAV navigation. A lightweight network encodes sparse observations into collision-risk-aware features using asymmetric and depthwise separable convolutions. We formulate the task as a constrained Markov decision process within a hierarchical control architecture and solve it using a Lagrangian-based safe PPO algorithm. Curriculum learning further improves training stability. Experiments with varying obstacle densities and flight speeds demonstrate higher success rates, improved safety, and better efficiency than existing reinforcement learning baselines.

### [15] [VLA-Corrector: Lightweight Detect-and-Correct Inference for Adaptive Action Horizon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01804)
*Yi Pan,Miao Pan,Qi Lu,Jiaming Huang,Man Zhang,Siteng Huang,Xin Li,Jie Zhang,Yongliang Shen,Xuhong Zhang,Wenqi Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: VLA-Corrector 是一种轻量级纠错推理框架，通过潜在空间视觉监控器和在线梯度引导，在不修改 VLA 主模型权重的情况下，实现事件触发的自适应动作视野，从而缓解动作分块策略中"预测后盲目执行"导致的复合误差问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 VLA 基础模型广泛采用动作分块机制——在固定动作视野下以开环方式执行多个未来动作。这种做法虽然降低了策略调用频率，但牺牲了闭环反应能力。在接触密集的物理交互中，开环盲区内的小扰动会迅速放大，产生复合误差并导致任务失败。为此，亟需一种不牺牲分块效率、同时恢复闭环纠错能力的机制。

Method: 提出 VLA-Corrector 框架，包含两个核心组件：(1) 轻量级潜在空间视觉监控器（LVM），持续对比预测视觉特征与实际视觉特征的演化，在线检测视觉动态偏差；(2) 在线梯度引导（OGG），一旦检测到持续性偏差，触发截断事件，丢弃剩余过期动作，并通过在线梯度引导调用纠错重规划。该"检测-纠错"机制自然形成事件触发的自适应动作视野：当前分块可靠时保持长视野执行，出现漂移时切换为短视野纠错重规划。

Result: VLA-Corrector 可集成到不同 VLA 模型中，无需对 VLA 骨干网络进行重新训练。在保持动作分块效率优势的同时，能够中断复合误差传播，显著提升长视野、接触密集的机器人操作任务的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: VLA-Corrector 通过事件触发自适应动作视野机制，成功打破了静态动作视野在执行鲁棒性与策略调用频率之间的固有权衡，在无需重训练 VLA 骨干的前提下，有效恢复了开环执行中的闭环纠错能力。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) foundation models have recently achieved strong progress in embodied intelligence. To reduce policy-call frequency while preserving temporal coherence, most generative policies adopt an action chunk mechanism, executing multiple future actions in an open-loop manner under a fixed action horizon. However, this "predict-then-blindly-execute" paradigm sacrifices closed-loop reactivity: in contact-rich physical interactions, even small local perturbations can rapidly amplify within the open-loop blind spot, leading to compounding errors and ultimately task failure. To address this limitation, we propose VLA-Corrector, a lightweight corrective inference framework for action-chunked VLA policies. Without modifying the backbone policy weights, VLA-Corrector introduces a lightweight Latent-space Vision Monitor (LVM) that continuously compares predicted and actual visual feature evolution, enabling online detection of visual dynamics deviations. Once persistent deviation is detected, the system triggers a truncation event, discards the remaining stale actions, and invokes corrective replanning via Online Gradient Guidance (OGG). The detect-and-correct mechanism of VLA-Corrector naturally induces an event-triggered adaptive action horizon: it preserves long-horizon execution when the current chunk remains reliable, and invokes short-horizon corrective replanning when execution begins to drift. In doing so, VLA-Corrector mitigates the trade-off imposed by static horizons between execution robustness and policy-call frequency. It can be integrated into different VLA models without further retraining the VLA backbone, interrupting compounding errors while preserving much of the efficiency benefit of action chunking and substantially improving robustness in long-horizon, contact-rich robotic manipulation tasks.

</details>


### [16] [DL-SLAM: Enabling High-Fidelity Gaussian Splatting SLAM in Dynamic Environments based on Dual-Level Probability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01860)
*Ziheng Xu,Qingfeng Li,Xuefeng Liu,Chen Chen,Jianwei Niu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: DL-SLAM 提出了一种基于双重概率框架的单目高斯泼溅SLAM系统，通过结合语义与几何信息计算像素级动态概率，并将其提升至物体级进行动态高斯的分类剪枝，从而消除静态地图中的伪影，同时提升追踪精度与语义地图质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动态SLAM方法通常直接丢弃预定义的动态物体，忽略了短暂静止物体对位姿估计的几何约束价值；而利用不确定性图的方法虽能利用这些物体，却将其错误地融入静态地图导致伪影，且纯几何信息造成物体边界模糊。

Method: 提出双重概率框架：首先融合语义与几何信息计算像素级动态概率图；然后将像素概率提升至3D并聚合为物体级动态概率；基于物体级概率对动态高斯进行分类剪枝，生成无伪影的静态地图；静态地图再反向为像素级概率提供几何一致性引导以增强其可靠性。

Result: 实验表明DL-SLAM优于现有方法，追踪精度提升最高达13%，并能生成高保真语义地图。

Conclusion: DL-SLAM通过双重概率框架有效解决了动态场景下静态地图伪影问题，同时利用短暂静止物体的几何约束显著提升了SLAM追踪精度。

Abstract: Recent advances in 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) have enabled significant progress in dense dynamic Simultaneous Localization And Mapping (SLAM). Prevailing methods typically discard predefined dynamic objects, ignoring that transiently static objects offer valuable geometric constraints for pose estimation. A recent work attempts to leverage this potential by employing per-pixel uncertainty maps to quantify the magnitude of motion. While this approach enables transiently static objects to enhance pose estimation, it erroneously integrates these objects into the static map, resulting in persistent artifacts. Moreover, its reliance on purely geometric information leads to ambiguous object boundaries in the uncertainty maps. To overcome these limitations, we present DL-SLAM, a monocular Gaussian Splatting SLAM system built upon a novel dual-level probabilistic framework. Our method computes dynamic probability maps by combining semantic and geometric information. These pixel-level probabilities are lifted to 3D and aggregated to derive an object-level dynamic probability for each instance. Object-level probability enables the categorical pruning of dynamic Gaussians, resulting in an artifact-free static map. The static map, in turn, provides a geometrically consistent guidance to refine the pixel-wise probabilities, enhancing their reliability. Experimental results demonstrate that DL-SLAM outperforms existing approaches, improving tracking accuracy by up to 13\% while generating high-fidelity semantic maps.

By explicitly accounting for the intricacies of pedestrian dynamics, the pipeline mitigates the reward bias and facilitates the systematic quantification of broad social norms, thereby fostering socially compliant behaviors. Extensive experiments integrating SPLC with offline RL methods demonstrate consistent improvements over state-of-the-art baselines across standard performance metrics. Furthermore, real-world experiments on the TurtleBot4 further validate the effectiveness of SPLC in practical human-robot coexistence settings. Our code and video demos are available at https://github.com/sklus949/SPLC.

Usual visual SLAM systems operating in dynamic environments often fail in the presence of moving objects, due to the static-world assumption used in pose estimation and mapping. To address this predicament, we introduce a novel geometric approach based on the discrepancy between disparity and a newly proposed notion called ``cross disparity'', which exploits both temporal and stereo inconsistency to identify dynamic feature points. Complementary to this feature-level motion analysis, OCD SLAM integrates a 3D object detection module (SMOKE) with Kalman filter-based object tracking to perform object-level motion classification, enabling robust separation of static and dynamic scene elements for accurate pose estimation. The proposed approach has been evaluated on various sequences from the KITTI Odometry and KITTI Raw datasets. Results demonstrate that OCD SLAM achieves significant improvement in trajectory accuracy compared to ORB-SLAM2 and several state-of-the-art dynamic SLAM methods. Ablation studies further demonstrate the effectiveness of the cross disparity module in the KITTI Raw dataset and show that this method is able to detect dynamic features that are missed by the 3D object detection scheme alone.

### [21] [Guided Action Flow: Q-Guided Inference for Flow-Matching Vision-Language-Action Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02092)
*Liuhaichen Yang,Zhuang Jiang,Chenchao Sheng,Zezhi Tang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出 Guided Action Flow，一种在推理时利用动作块评论家（action-chunk critic）引导冻结的流匹配 VLA 策略采样的框架。在 LIBERO 操作任务上，该方法显著提升了单任务成功率，多任务场景也有正向但有限的增益，揭示评论家泛化与不确定性感知引导是核心瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流匹配 VLA（Vision-Language-Action）策略通过迭代传输过程生成动作块，这为无需重新训练基策略的测试时引导创造了条件。然而，如何在不修改预训练策略权重的前提下，利用成功/失败 rollout 数据进一步提升策略表现，是一个开放问题。

Method: 提出 Guided Action Flow 框架：(1) 保持预训练的 SmolVLA 策略完全冻结；(2) 利用真实成功与失败 rollout 数据训练一个动作块评论家（action-chunk critic），该评论家可条件化于来自冻结 SmolVLA 语言通路的任务描述特征；(3) 在逆向流采样过程中，仅通过动作梯度使用该评论家进行引导，无需修改策略权重。

Result: 在 LIBERO 操作任务上，单任务评论家将成功率从一个种子窗口的 68.0% 提升至 82.0%，另一窗口从 82.0% 提升至 86.0%。多家族任务描述评论家将验证成功率从 46.0% 提升至 56.0%，但锁定留出测试集的增益较为温和，仅从 65.0% 提升至 67.5%。

Conclusion: 结果表明，Q 引导推理对冻结的流匹配 VLA 策略是可行的，但评论家的泛化能力和不确定性感知引导仍是当前的核心瓶颈，值得进一步研究。

Abstract: Flow-matching vision-language-action policies generate robot action chunks through an iterative transport process, creating an opportunity for test-time guidance without retraining the base policy. We study this opportunity in Guided Action Flow, an inference-time framework that keeps a pretrained SmolVLA policy frozen and uses a learned action-chunk critic to guide its reverse-time flow sampler. The critic is trained from real success and failure rollouts, can condition on task-description features from the frozen SmolVLA language pathway, and is used only through action gradients during sampling. We evaluate the approach on LIBERO manipulation tasks. A single-task critic improves success from 68.0% to 82.0% on one seed window and from 82.0% to 86.0% on another. A multi-family task-description critic improves validation success from 46.0% to 56.0%, while the locked held-out test gain is positive but modest, from 65.0% to 67.5%. These results support the feasibility of Q-guided inference for frozen flow-matching VLA policies, while showing that critic generalization and uncertainty-aware guidance remain the central bottlenecks.

Abstract: Robotic choreography in open water is governed by nonlinear fluid dynamics, which impose significant challenges due to environmental disturbances and nonlinear system dynamics. This paper presents the cyber-physical architecture of Way of Water, a vertically integrated framework that orchestrates a fleet of autonomous surface vessels as a distributed choreographic platform. Moving beyond the surface-pixel paradigm, these vessels use laminar nozzles and multi-zone lighting to extend their expressive range from the 2D water plane into the 3D volumetric domain. Our primary contribution is the Way of Water Studio, a browser-based, timeline-compositing authoring paradigm that treats the fleet as a DAW-like instrument for music-responsive choreography. The Studio encapsulates Sequential Convex Programming for trajectory generation and Model Predictive Control for disturbance rejection presented through a visual timeline, broadening access to high-performance aquatic robotics for non-programmer artists. Grounding the Studio is the full cyber-physical stack: a custom holonomic chassis, a state-estimation and control stack tuned for the aquatic domain, and an LTE/MQTT fleet link with RTK-GPS time synchronization. We report on the system's validation across two distinct deployments: an 18-vessel Swan Lake interpretation at Lake Zurich and an 8-vessel Time Space Existence 2025 Venice Biennale demonstration at Forte Marghera, establishing a foundational reference for the design and deployment of fluidic robotic swarms.

### [23] [Bridge-WA: Predicting Where and How the World Changes for Robotic Action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02195)
*Yongjie Bai,Hanting Wang,Mingtong Dai,Qijun Zhong,Yang Liu,Liang Lin*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Bridge-WA 提出了一种轻量级的世界-动作框架，通过将冻结的未来变化教师模型蒸馏为三种紧凑先验（未来 tokens、变化图、运动流图），并通过 WorldBridge 条件化动作 Transformer，在不依赖推理时密集未来图像生成的情况下，显著提升了机器人操作在分布外场景下的泛化能力和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界-动作模型依赖大型生成式世界模型或密集未来 rollout，计算开销大，且将大量容量浪费在与控制弱相关的视觉细节上。作者希望找到一种更高效的方式，将动作相关的场景变化先验注入策略学习，同时避免推理时的高成本未来生成。

Method: Bridge-WA 框架包含三阶段：(1) 利用冻结的未来变化教师模型提取三种紧凑先验——未来 tokens（表征预期结果）、变化图（支持干预）、运动流图（局部转移方向）；(2) 设计 WorldBridge 模块，通过多源注意力记忆和时空偏置将上述先验条件化注入动作 Transformer；(3) 推理时移除教师模型，仅保留轻量先验与 WorldBridge，避免密集未来图像生成。

Result: 在 VLABench、RoboTwin2.0、LIBERO-Plus 和真实机器人评估中，Bridge-WA 在任务成功率、完成进度和鲁棒性上均有提升；尤其在分布外视觉偏移（背景、光照、干扰物变化）下，优势更为显著。

Conclusion: 通过将动作生成聚焦于场景"何处变化"和"如何变化"，Bridge-WA 有效抑制了与外观相关的干扰因素，实现了更好的泛化能力，且无需在部署时进行密集未来图像生成，是一种高效且鲁棒的世界-动作学习范式。

Abstract: General-purpose vision-language-action models benefit from large vision-language priors, but effective manipulation also requires anticipating action-relevant scene changes. Existing world-action models often rely on large generative world models or dense future rollouts, which are expensive and spend capacity on visual details weakly coupled to control. We present Bridge-WA, a lightweight world-action framework that distills a frozen future-change teacher into three compact priors: future tokens for intended outcomes, change maps for intervention support, and motion-flow maps for local transition direction. A WorldBridge conditions the action transformer on these priors through multi-source attention memories and spatial-temporal biases, while the teacher model is removed at inference. Across VLABench, RoboTwin2.0, LIBERO-Plus and real-robot evaluations, Bridge-WA improves task success, progress, and robustness, with particularly clear gains under out-of-distribution visual shifts. By focusing action generation on where and how the scene will change, Bridge-WA suppresses nuisance appearance factors such as background, lighting, and distractors, leading to better generalization without deployment-time dense future-image generation. Code and visualizations are available at: https://hcplab-sysu.github.io/BRIDGE-WA .

</details>


### [24] [Actuator Reality Shaping for Zero-Shot Sim-to-Real Robot Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02205)
*Satoshi Yamamori,Koji Ishihara,Kentaro Minamikawa,Kiyoharu Ohomori,Taiyo Yazaki,Norikazu Sugimoto,Jun Morimoto*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出"执行器现实塑形"（Actuator Reality Shaping）方法：不修改仿真器去匹配真实世界，而是通过二自由度前馈-反馈控制器，将物理执行器的闭环行为塑形为与仿真中使用的理想二阶参考动力学一致，从而实现强化学习策略的零样本 sim-to-real 迁移，并在单关节伺服系统、7-DOF 机械臂、轮腿机器人和人形机器人上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人学习中的 sim-to-real 迁移常受限于仿真中理想的执行器动力学假设与物理电机非线性、硬件依赖行为之间的偏差。传统方法（系统辨识、域随机化、学习执行器模型）均试图让仿真逼近现实，但仿真精度的提升存在上限且成本高昂。本文反其道而行，提出让现实执行器去匹配理想的仿真参考模型，从根本上消除 sim-to-real 的执行器动力学失配问题。

Method: 核心方法是为每个关节配备二自由度（2-DOF）前馈-反馈控制器。前馈通道负责参考响应塑形（使闭环系统呈现预设的理想二阶参考动力学），反馈通道则专门处理鲁棒镇定和扰动抑制，两者解耦设计。由此，物理执行器对外呈现标准化、可预定义的动力学接口。强化学习策略仅需在仿真中用该参考模型训练，即可直接部署到物理硬件上。方法无需任务级微调，也无需学习执行器模型。

Result: 在外部负载下的单关节高减速比伺服系统上验证了底层跟踪性能；在 7-DOF 机械臂到达任务中，相比标准伺服控制和代表性的 real-to-sim-to-real 基线方法，执行器现实塑形显著降低了 sim-to-real 跟踪误差，提升了零样本任务性能；进一步在轮腿机器人坡面行驶和人形机器人行走任务上展示了零样本迁移能力。

Conclusion: 执行器现实塑形提供了一种可复用的标准化执行器接口范式，使强化学习策略无需感知底层硬件差异即可实现零样本 sim-to-real 迁移，有望成为跨多样化机器人平台的通用解决方案。

Abstract: Sim-to-real transfer in robot learning is often limited by discrepancies between the ideal actuator dynamics assumed during policy training and the nonlinear, hardware-dependent behavior of physical motors. While conventional approaches attempt to bridge this gap by increasing simulator fidelity through system identification, domain randomization, or learned actuator models, we introduce an alternative paradigm: actuator reality shaping. Instead of modifying the simulator to match the real world, our method shapes the closed-loop behavior of physical actuators to match the idealized second-order reference dynamics used in simulation. By equipping each joint with a two-degree-of-freedom feedforward--feedback controller, we decouple reference-response shaping from robust stabilization, thereby providing a standardized actuator interface for reinforcement learning policies. As a result, policies trained only with the prescribed reference model can be deployed zero-shot on real hardware without task-level fine-tuning or learned actuator models. We validate the approach on a single-joint high-gear-ratio servo under external loads and a 7-DOF robotic arm reaching task, where actuator reality shaping substantially reduces sim-to-real tracking error and improves zero-shot task performance compared with standard servo-control and representative real-to-sim-to-real baselines. We further demonstrate zero-shot transfer on a wheeled-legged robot driving over a slope and a humanoid robot walking, suggesting that actuator reality shaping can serve as a reusable interface for robot learning across diverse hardware platforms.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLN 领域过度关注高层指令推理、记忆和地图构建，低层动作表示研究不足；现有离散动作（前进+转弯）限制了连续控制与闭环比较。

Method: 将 VLN-CE 片段转换为帧级局部监督（对齐子指令、动作、轨迹、密集流场目标）；CoFL-S 预测机器人局部可见扇区的语言条件化流场，通过 rollout 生成连续轨迹；引入连续时间 Habitat 基准，通过共享速度指令控制器实现分解无关的闭环比较。

Result: 在匹配编码器和训练设置下，CoFL-S 在不同规划频率下均一致优于 action-token 和 action-chunk 基线；零样本真实世界闭环部署进一步验证其优势。

Conclusion: 低层连续动作表示（语言条件化流场）对 VLN 至关重要，CoFL-S 在仿真和真实环境中均展现显著优势。

Abstract: Vision-Language Navigation has increasingly emphasized high-level instruction reasoning, memory, global map construction, and instruction decomposition, while the low-level action representation remains comparatively underexplored. We propose CoFL-S, a low-level vision-language-action framework that predicts a language-conditioned flow field over the robot's local visible sector and generates continuous trajectories by rolling out the predicted field. To train this low-level representation, we convert each VLN-CE episode, originally a whole-episode instruction paired with an action sequence, into frame-level local supervision with aligned sub-instructions and matched action, trajectory, and dense flow-field targets. For evaluation, we introduce a continuous-time Habitat benchmark that isolates low-level action interfaces from instruction decomposition and executes all methods through a shared velocity-command controller, enabling decomposition-independent closed-loop comparison across different planner frequencies rather than fixed discrete forward-and-turn transitions in VLN-CE. Under matched encoders and training settings, CoFL-S consistently outperforms action-token and action-chunk baselines across planner frequencies in the continuous-time Habitat benchmark, and zero-shot real-world closed-loop deployment further shows its advantage over both baselines beyond simulation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

We present NEUROSYMLAND, a neuro-symbolic landing-site assessment system that integrates lightweight perception with explicit safety reasoning. The framework constructs a probabilistic semantic scene graph from onboard visual input and evaluates candidate landing regions using symbolic constraints capturing terrain flatness, obstacle clearance, and spatial consistency, enabling structured reasoning under perceptual uncertainty while maintaining edge-feasible execution. Across 72 simulated landing scenarios spanning diverse terrains, NEUROSYMLAND achieves 61 successful assessments, outperforming four competitive baselines (37-57 successes). To evaluate deployability, we further conduct 100 hardware-in-the-loop trials with randomized initial poses, profiling end-to-end latency, stage-wise execution time, and system-level metrics including CPU/GPU utilization, memory footprint, and power consumption. Results demonstrate improved robustness and interpretability with bounded edge-resource usage. Profiling shows that symbolic reasoning contributes only a small fraction of end-to-end latency, while the main computational cost arises from perception and PSSG construction. These results demonstrate the feasibility of deploying the landing-site assessment stack on edge-constrained UAV hardware, and all source code, datasets, prompts, and symbolic rule refinement examples are released in an open-source repository

### [28] [The Moving Eye: Enhancing VLA Spatial Generalization via Hybrid Dynamic Data Collection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02322)
*Jincheng Tang,Yilong Zhu,Zhengyuan Xie,Jiang-Jiang Liu,Jiaxing Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该文针对VLA模型空间泛化能力脆弱的根源——捷径学习（依赖伪相关而非真实空间关系），提出一种基于双臂系统（一臂操作、一臂作为移动环境相机）的混合数据采集策略，结合连续相机运动与多样化静态视角，有效消除伪相关、提升空间泛化能力，且该策略对ACT、Diffusion、Pi0、Gr00t等多种架构均有显著增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLA模型在机器人操作中空间泛化能力差，仅增加视角数量无法解决根本问题。核心症结在于模型陷入捷径学习（Shortcut Learning），即模型捕捉的是物体间或相机与机器人基座间的固定相对位姿等伪相关，而非学习真正的空间关系。因此需要一种数据层面的解决方案来系统性地消除这些伪相关。

Method: 采用双臂实验平台，一臂执行操作任务，另一臂充当移动环境相机。系统性地评估了三种数据分布模式：(1) Fixed——固定视角；(2) Multi-Fixed——多个固定视角；(3) Moving Views——连续运动视角。最终提出一种混合策略，将连续相机运动与多样化静态视角相结合，在降低伪相关的同时保持训练稳定性。实验验证该策略在未见过的相机位姿和物体配置上的泛化表现。

Result: 混合策略（连续相机运动 + 多样化静态视角）在所有方案中表现最优，能够显著减少伪相关，使VLA模型成功泛化到未见相机位姿和物体配置。相比之下，单纯增加静态视角无法解决泛化问题。此外，捷径学习易感性和空间泛化困难是跨架构的普遍特性，ACT、Diffusion Policy、Pi0、Gr00t等模型均从该混合数据策略中获得显著提升。

Conclusion: 提升VLA空间泛化的关键不在于简单增加数据量或视角数，而在于通过数据分布设计主动打破伪相关。混合连续运动与静态视角的数据采集策略是一种通用、架构无关的解决方案，对多类主流机器人操作模型均有普适的增益效果。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown remarkable promise in generalized robotic manipulation. However, their spatial generalization remains fragile. We argue that simply increasing the number of viewpoints is insufficient. Models often fall into the trap of Shortcut Learning, latching onto spurious correlations (e.g., fixed relative poses between objects or between the camera and robot base) rather than learning true spatial relationships. In this work, we propose a data-centric solution to enhance VLA spatial generalization. We utilize a dual-arm setup where one arm performs manipulation while the other serves as a mobile environmental camera. We systematically evaluate three data distribution patterns: Fixed, Multi-Fixed, and Moving Views. Our findings reveal that a hybrid strategy, combining continuous camera motion with diverse static viewpoints, yields the best performance by substantially reducing spurious correlations while maintaining training stability. Our experiments demonstrate that this strategy mitigates spurious correlations, enabling VLAs to generalize to unseen camera poses and object configurations where simply adding more static viewpoints fails. Crucially, we reveal that the susceptibility to shortcut learning and the struggle with spatial generalization are universal characteristics shared across diverse architectures. Consequently, all evaluated models (ACT, Diffusion, and VLA models including Pi0 and Gr00t) benefit significantly from our mixed data strategy.

Method: 提出HEFT框架，包含两大核心组件：（1）**特权运动引导（PMG）**：从带噪声的VR参考数据中重建物理合理的参考运动，用于策略学习；（2）**窗口化负载课程（WPC）**：采用专家引导的负载上限，逐步增加负载以获取稳健的重载跟踪能力。部署于175cm、65kg的L7人形机器人上。

We present HEFT, a heavy-payload full-size humanoid teleoperation framework that addresses both challenges. HEFT learns from deployable noisy VR references with physically plausible reconstructed references through Privileged Motion Guidance (PMG), and uses a Windowed Payload Curriculum (WPC) with expert-guided payload caps to acquire robust heavy-payload tracking. ### [30] [ACID: Action Consistency via Inverse Dynamics for Planning with World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02403)
*Gawon Seo,Dongwon Kim,Suha Kwak*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: ACID 提出在决策时规划中引入循环动作一致性约束，通过逆动力学模型验证前向预测轨迹的可实现性，并用尺度不变的自适应权重将逐帧残差纳入规划代价，在多种世界模型和任务上一致提升规划效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于动作条件世界模型的决策时规划方法仅以预测终端状态与目标的接近程度来评判候选轨迹，忽略了中间过渡状态的可实现性——预测轨迹可能在视觉上合理，但实际环境执行会逐渐偏离。需要一种能检验中间步骤可实现性的机制。

Method: 提出 ACID 框架，核心是循环动作一致性：对每个预测的状态转移，用逆动力学模型反向推断动作，要求该动作与原始条件动作一致。将每步的动作残差通过尺度不变的自适应权重纳入规划代价函数中，实现对轨迹全局和局部可实现性的联合评估。

Result: 在四种动作条件世界模型（包括扩散模型、Transformer 等）和六类任务（刚体/可变形体操作、关节体控制、视觉导航）上，ACID 一致提升规划性能，且用显著更少的规划计算量即可达到基线方法的准确率。

Conclusion: 循环动作一致性是一种通用、轻量的规划代价增强策略，可即插即用于多种世界模型和任务，在不增加模型训练的前提下提升决策时规划的可靠性与效率。

Abstract: Decision-time planning with action-conditioned world models has become a popular paradigm for embodied control. However, the standard planning cost judges a candidate solely by how close its predicted terminal state lies to the goal, leaving the realizability of the intermediate transitions unchecked -- a predicted trajectory can look convincing while the environment rollout drifts away from it. In this paper, we propose ACID, a decision-time planning framework that introduces cycle action consistency: the action inferred backward from a predicted transition by an inverse dynamics model should recover the one that was conditioned on. We fold this per-step residual into the planning cost via a scale-invariant adaptive weight. Across four action-conditioned world models and six tasks spanning rigid and deformable manipulation, articulated control, and visual navigation, ACID consistently improves planning and matches the baseline's accuracy with substantially less planning compute.

</details>


### [31] [LIME: Learning Intent-aware Camera Motion from Egocentric Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02417)
*Boyang Sun,Jiajie Li,Yung-Hsu Yang,Chenyangguang Zhang,Tim Engelbracht,Sunghwan Hong,Cesar Cadena,Marc Pollefeys,Hermann Blum*

TL;DR: 本文研究语言条件驱动的相机运动生成任务：给定当前RGB观测和自由形式自然语言意图，预测相对目标相机位姿。作者从自我中心视频中挖掘多意图相机运动监督信号，并提出LIME模型，结合自回归观测增益输出与连续流匹配位姿头，实现意图感知的主动感知。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主机器人经常需要主动移动相机来执行检查、揭示遮挡区域或响应用户意图，但语言条件驱动的相机运动作为一类独立动作尚未被充分探索。现有视觉语言导航和操控策略分别处理基座运动和操作，唯独缺少对相机运动这一动作原语的系统建模。

Method: 提出LIME（Language-Informed caMera movEment）模型：(1) 从自我中心视频中挖掘多意图相机运动监督，将合理意图和观测增益描述与相对SE(3)目标位姿配对；(2) 模型架构结合自回归观测增益输出（预测下一视图应揭示什么）与连续流匹配位姿头（表示多假设目标视图）。

Result: 实验表明，LIME能够从被动人类视频中学习主动选择相机位姿，将普通自我中心视频转化为意图感知主动感知的监督信号，并在下游机器人任务中验证了有效性。

Conclusion: 语言条件相机运动生成是一项有挑战性但可行的任务，通过挖掘被动视频中的多意图监督并结合自回归增益预测与流匹配，可以实现从自然语言意图到相机位姿的有效映射，为机器人主动感知提供了新的方法框架。

Abstract: Autonomous robots often need to move their camera before they can act: to inspect an object, reveal an occluded region, or obtain a view that responds to a user's intent. While vision-language navigation translates instructions to base motion and vision-language-action policies map instructions to manipulation actions, language-conditioned camera motion remains comparatively underexplored as a first-class action. We formulate language-conditioned camera motion generation: given a current RGB observation and a free-form natural-language intent, predict a relative target camera pose for the next observation. This task is inherently non-trivial: viewpoint changes are driven by latent perceptual intentions, and a valid motion may operate at different semantic granularity, from entering a room to looking around a corner, inspecting a visible object, or revealing an occluded detail. To model this structure, we mine multi-intention camera-motion supervision from egocentric video, pairing plausible intents and observation-gain descriptions with relative SE(3) target poses. We propose LIME, a vision-language camera-motion generator that combines an auto-regressive observation-gain output with a continuous flow-matching pose head. This design lets the model jointly predict what the next view should reveal while representing multi-hypothesis target views. Across experiments and downstream robotic tasks, we show that LIME can learn to actively choose camera poses from passive human video, turning ordinary egocentric recordings into supervision for intent-aware active perception.

</details>


### [32] [WorldSample: Closed-loop Real-robot RL with World Modelling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02431)
*Yuquan Xue,Le Xu,Zeyi Liu,Zhenyu Wu,Zhengyi Gu,Xinyang Song,Bofang Jia,Ziwei Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: WorldSample提出一种面向真实机器人强化学习的物理数据增强框架，通过真实数据采集与世界模型生成形成闭环，结合策略步调学习（PPL）调节训练过程，在接触丰富和精确操作任务中将成功率提升28%、训练步数减少59%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实机器人强化学习面临两大困境：模仿学习受限于示范覆盖范围，而强化学习虽能通过试错突破此限制，但真实环境中的物理 rollout 成本极高，每次仅获得单一行动-结果路径。需要一种低成本、高保真的数据增强方法来解决这一效率瓶颈。

Method: 提出WorldSample框架，包含三个核心环节：(1) 在真实rollout基础上，通过后训练世界模型生成高保真合成转移，显著降低视觉幻觉；(2) 构建「真实-合成闭环」，使世界模型与策略交替迭代提升；(3) 引入策略步调学习（Policy-Paced Learning, PPL），通过样本选择与调度机制，在利用合成数据增强与抑制价值高估/幻觉噪声之间取得平衡。

Result: 在接触丰富和精确操作的机器人操控任务上，WorldSample相比基线方法将策略成功率提升28%，训练步数减少59%；世界模型视觉保真度方面，PSNR提升19.4dB，SSIM提升0.47，验证了真实-合成闭环对策略和世界模型的双向增益。

Conclusion: WorldSample通过真实-合成闭环有效解决了真实机器人RL中数据效率低和交互成本高的难题，PPL机制在利用合成数据的同时缓解了价值高估和幻觉噪声问题，为真实机器人强化学习提供了一种实用且高效的数据增强范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) can overcome the demonstration-coverage limitation of imitation learning (IL) by allowing robots to improve through trial-and-error interaction beyond the states observed in demonstrations. However, deploying RL on real robots remains constrained by high interaction costs, since each physical rollout is costly and reflects only one realized action-outcome path. To address this challenge, we propose WorldSample, a physically grounded data augmentation framework for real-robot RL that closes a real-synthetic loop between physical rollouts, world-model generation, and policy improvement. Grounded on real rollouts, WorldSample generates high-fidelity synthetic transitions through a post-trained world model, which greatly lowers the visual hallucination. Specifically, rather than simply using these transitions as real-world experience, WorldSample introduces Policy-Paced Learning (PPL) to regulate the training process through sample selection and scheduling, balancing useful augmentation against value overestimation and mitigating the hallucination-induced noise. Experiments on robot manipulation tasks involving contact-rich and precise tasks show that WorldSample improves policy success rate by 28% while reducing training steps by 59% compared with baselines. Furthermore, WorldSample improves world model visual fidelity by 19.4dB in PSNR and 0.47 in SSIM over demonstration-only post-training, validating the effectiveness of the real-synthetic loop for both policy and world model performance.

### [33] [Learning to Move Before Learning to Do: Task-Agnostic pretraining for VLAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02466)
*Junhao Shi,Siyin Wang,Xiaopeng Yu,Li Ji,Jingjing Gong,Xipeng Qiu*

Main category: cs.RO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA模型受限于专家演示数据（观测-指令-动作三元组）的稀缺和高昂采集成本。作者认为这一瓶颈源于将两种不同学习目标混为一谈：物理能力（如何移动）和语义对齐（做什么），其中仅后者需要语言监督。

Method: 提出TAP两阶段框架：第一阶段通过自监督逆动力学（Inverse Dynamics）目标，从廉价的无标签交互数据（包括被丢弃的离轨轨迹和自主机器人玩耍数据）中学习可迁移的运动先验；第二阶段使用极少量专家标注数据，将这些运动先验与语言指令进行对齐。

Result: 在SIMPLER基准上，TAP匹配了使用超100万条专家轨迹训练的模型性能，且标注数据量少数个数量级，相比标准行为克隆获得10%的绝对提升。在真实WidowX平台上，当相机受到扰动时TAP保持25%成功率，而互联网规模基线模型成功率降至0%。

Conclusion: 任务无关预训练能产生鲁棒、可迁移的物理表征，验证了分解假说的有效性，为具身AI提供了一条可扩展的路径。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are fundamentally bottlenecked by the scarcity of expert demonstrations -- triplets of observations, instructions, and actions that are costly to collect at scale. We argue that this bottleneck stems from conflating two distinct learning objectives: acquiring physical competence (how to move) and acquiring semantic alignment (what to do). Crucially, only the latter requires language supervision. Building on this Decomposition Hypothesis, we propose Task-Agnostic Pretraining (TAP), a two-stage framework that first learns transferable motor priors from cheap, unlabeled interaction data -- including discarded off-task trajectories and autonomous robot play -- via a self-supervised Inverse Dynamics objective. A lightweight second stage then grounds these priors in language using minimal expert data. On the SIMPLER benchmark, TAP matches models trained on over 1M expert trajectories while using orders of magnitude less labeled data, yielding a 10% absolute gain over standard behavior cloning. On a real-world WidowX platform, TAP retains 25% success under camera perturbations where internet-scale baselines collapse to 0%, demonstrating that task-agnostic pretraining produces robust, transferable physical representations and offers a scalable path forward for Embodied AI.

### [35] [QuadRocket: An Aerial Robotic Testbed for Adaptive Thrust-Vector Control of Rocket-Like Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02474)
*Pedro Santos,Joel Reis,Paulo Oliveira,Carlos Silvestre*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: QuadRocket 是一种四旋翼火箭原型平台，由一个四旋翼通过万向节支撑圆柱形机体，构成飞行倒立摆。论文基于轴对称刚体模型，采用双球面上的降维姿态表示，设计了自适应反步控制器实现全局轨迹跟踪，并通过动态面姿态控制器将四旋翼作为推力矢量执行器。仿真与室内实验验证了其轨迹跟踪精度和扰动补偿能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为运载火箭类系统的先进推力矢量控制策略验证提供低成本、低风险的实验平台。传统火箭验证成本高、风险大，需要一种可重复使用、室内可飞的替代方案。

Method: 1) 系统建模：将四旋翼与圆柱机体耦合系统建模为单轴对称刚体，推力沿纵轴施加；2) 姿态表示：采用 S² 球面上的降维姿态表示，利用轴向对称性解耦偏航与推力矢量方向；3) 控制器设计：推导自适应反步控制器实现几乎全局轨迹跟踪，结合控制点变换缓解非最小相位行为；4) 执行器层：将四旋翼视为推力矢量执行器，设计基于动态面的姿态控制器跟踪期望推力矢量，避免虚拟控制信号的显式微分。

Result: 仿真和室内运动捕捉场地的实验验证表明：所提架构实现了精确的轨迹跟踪和有效的扰动补偿，证实 QuadRocket 可作为推力矢量控制机器人飞行器的多功能测试平台。

Conclusion: QuadRocket 为推力矢量控制策略验证提供了一种低成本、低风险且有效的实验平台，自适应反步控制与动态面控制的层级架构在轨迹跟踪和抗扰动方面表现优异。

Abstract: This paper presents QuadRocket, a quadrotor-based rocket prototype that provides a low-cost, low-risk platform for validating advanced thrust-vector control strategies for launch vehicle-type systems. The prototype consists of a cylindrical main body mounted on top of a quadrotor through a universal joint, forming a flying inverted pendulum with non-negligible inertia. For control design, the coupled system is modeled as a single axisymmetric rigid body actuated by a vectored force applied along its longitudinal axis. A reduced-attitude representation on the two sphere is adopted to explicitly exploit the vehicle's axial symmetry and to decouple yaw from the thrust-vector direction. On this model, we derive an adaptive backstepping controller that achieves almost global trajectory tracking in the presence of unknown constant disturbances, while a control-point transformation mitigates non minimum-phase behavior. The quadrotor is then treated as a thrust vector actuator, and a dynamic-surface-based attitude controller is designed to track the desired thrust-vector, accounting for actuation dynamics and avoiding explicit differentiation of virtual control signals. The complete architecture is evaluated in simulation and validated experimentally in an indoor motion-capture arena. Results demonstrate accurate trajectory tracking, effective disturbance compensation, and confirm the suitability of the QuadRocket as a versatile testbed for thrust-vector-controlled robotic vehicles.

### [36] [Controllable Sim Agents with Behavior Latents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02496)
*Juanwu Lu,Junyu Zhu,Ziran Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: CNeVA 提出了一种可控的交通智能体仿真框架，通过共轭变分推断学习每智能体高斯行为隐变量，结合整流流轨迹生成器和混合通道掩码课程训练，实现沿多轴（速度、加速度、安全性、地图合规性）可操控的逼真交通仿真。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有逼真交通仿真模型缺乏可操控性（controllability），工程师无法沿可解释的轴（如速度、安全性）操纵智能体行为，从而难以隔离变量、复现边缘场景和测试自主系统。同时，奖励信号稀疏（只有少数智能体有显著回报）导致训练困难。

Method: 1. 使用共轭变分更新（conjugate variational update）从每通道折扣回报中推断每智能体的高斯行为隐变量；2. 训练整流流（rectified-flow）轨迹生成器，采用混合通道掩码课程实现无分类器引导（classifier-free guidance）；3. 提出软资格门（soft eligibility gates），用平滑指数衰减替代硬二值阈值，保留近阈值智能体的梯度信号；4. 引入上下文残差回报度量（context-residual return measure）实现可操控的地图合规性。

Result: 在 Waymo Open Motion Dataset 上，CNeVA 达到有竞争力的逼真度，同时暴露排名更高的纯模仿模型所缺乏的逐通道可操控性；速度和加速度操控产生单调响应且无停滞式奖励黑客现象；引入软资格门后安全性操控单调且显著；成功实现可操控的地图合规性；实验表明操控指标须结合物理合理性护栏以避免奖励黑客混淆。

Conclusion: CNeVA 在保持逼真度竞争力的前提下实现了多通道可操控性，软资格门有效缓解奖励稀疏问题，且操控评估必须与物理合理性指标联合使用才能避免被奖励黑客行为误导。

Abstract: Realistic traffic simulation requires agents that imitate logged behavior and can also be steered along interpretable axes. Such controllability enables engineers to isolate variables, reproduce specific edge cases, and test autonomous systems without real-world risk. We introduce Controllable Neural Variational Agents (CNeVA), a controllable simulated-agent framework that learns to infer a per-agent Gaussian behavior latent from per-channel discounted returns via a closed-form conjugate variational update, conditioning a rectified-flow trajectory generator trained on a mixed channel-mask curriculum for classifier-free guidance. To tackle scarcity in reward signals, we propose soft eligibility gates that replace hard binary thresholds with smooth exponential decay, preserving the gradient signal for near-threshold agents. On the Waymo Open Motion Dataset, CNeVA attains competitive realism on the benchmark while exposing per-channel controllability that the higher-ranked imitation models lack. Speed- and acceleration-based steering produces monotone responses without stall-induced reward hacking. Safety controllability is monotone and substantial with the introduction of soft eligibility. We manage to achieve steerable map compliance under a context-residual return measure. Furthermore, our experiment demonstrates that steering metrics must be read alongside physical-plausibility guardrails to avoid reward-hacking confounds.

### [37] [Embodied.cpp: A Portable Inference Runtime of Embodied AI Models on Heterogeneous Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02501)
*Ling Xu,Chuyu Han,Borui Li,Hao Wu,Shiqi Jiang,Ting Cao,Chuanyou Li,Sheng Zhong,Shuai Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Embodied.cpp是一个可移植的C++推理运行时，专为具身AI模型（VLA和WAM）设计，解决了现有推理框架在边缘设备闭环控制、低延迟批量-1推理和可扩展接口方面的不足。通过五层模块化架构，在HY-VLA和pi0.5上分别达到100%和91%的任务成功率，并将WAM块内存从312.2 MiB降至88.1 MiB。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA和WAM等具身AI模型在实际部署中面临碎片化问题：各模型依赖特定的Python技术栈、后端假设和机器人端胶水代码，尤其是异构边缘设备。当前推理运行时主要面向请求-响应服务模式，无法满足具身部署的三个核心需求：闭环控制中的多速率执行、异构硬件上的延迟优先批量-1推理，以及超越固定token I/O的可扩展具身接口。

Method: 作者提出Embodied.cpp——一个可移植C++推理运行时。通过对代表性VLA模型和WAM进行架构分析，捕捉共享执行路径，将其组织为五层架构：输入适配器(Input Adapters)、序列构建器(Sequence Builders)、骨干执行(Backbone Execution)、头部插件(Head Plugins)和部署适配器(Deployment Adapters)。该运行时提供模块化多速率执行、延迟优先融合推理，以及可扩展的算子和I/O支持，通过统一后端抽象实现跨异构设备、机器人和仿真器的部署。

Result: 在两个VLA模型HY-VLA和pi0.5上实现闭环执行，任务成功率分别为100.0%和91.0%。在基于LingBot-VA Transformer块的初步WAM基准测试中，块内存从312.2 MiB降至88.1 MiB（降低约71.8%）。

Conclusion: Embodied.cpp在保持多样化具身模型架构高准确率的同时，显著提升了部署效率，验证了其作为统一具身推理运行时的有效性。

Abstract: Embodied AI models now span vision-language-action (VLA) models and world-action models (WAMs), but practical deployment remains fragmented across model-specific Python stacks, backend assumptions, and robot-side glue code, especially on heterogeneous edge devices. Existing inference runtimes are designed mainly for request-response serving and therefore do not satisfy the runtime contract of embodied deployment: multi-rate execution inside closed-loop control, latency-first batch-1 inference on heterogeneous hardware, and extensible embodied interfaces beyond fixed token I/O. We present Embodied.cpp, a portable C++ inference runtime for embodied models. Based on an architectural analysis of representative VLA models and WAMs, Embodied.cpp captures a shared execution path and organizes it into five layers: input adapters, sequence builders, backbone execution, head plugins, and deployment adapters. The runtime provides modular multi-rate execution, latency-first fused inference, and extensible operator and I/O support, enabling deployment across heterogeneous devices, robots, and simulators through one backend abstraction. We evaluate Embodied.cpp on two VLA models, HY-VLA and pi0.5, and on a preliminary WAM benchmark using a LingBot-VA Transformer block. The VLA deployments achieve successful closed-loop execution with 100.0% and 91.0% task success rates, respectively. The WAM benchmark reduces block memory from 312.2 MiB to 88.1 MiB. These results show that Embodied.cpp improves deployment efficiency while preserving high accuracy across diverse embodied model architectures.

### [38] [VT-WAM: Visual-Tactile World Action Model for Contact-Rich Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02503)
*Shuai Tian,Yupeng Zheng,Yuhang Zheng,Songen Gu,Yujie Zang,Yuxing Qin,Weize Li,Haoran Li,Wenchao Ding,Dongbin Zhao*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: VT-WAM 提出一种视觉-触觉世界动作模型，在统一的流匹配框架中联合学习未来视觉预测、触觉形变预测和动作预测，通过非对称混合Transformer注意力和接触门控注意力引导机制，在六项真实接触丰富操作任务中显著超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 接触丰富操作需要策略对局部形变、压力、滑动和摩擦等触觉线索做出反应，但这些线索时间稀疏且视觉难以观测。现有视觉-触觉策略通常直接馈入触觉观测进行动作预测，很少在动作生成过程中显式建模触觉形变动力学。

Method: 提出VT-WAM，在统一的流匹配框架中联合学习视觉预测、触觉形变预测和动作预测。包含两个关键设计：(1) 非对称混合Transformer（Asymmetric MoT）注意力，将首帧视觉锚点与时序触觉动力学桥接；(2) 接触门控的动作-视觉-触觉注意力引导（AVTAG），在接触阶段鼓励动作查询依赖触觉证据。

Result: 在六项真实世界接触丰富操作任务中，VT-WAM达到71.67%的平均成功率，比Fast-WAM高26.67%，比OmniVTLA高35.84%。消融实验验证了建模触觉形变动力学和引导接触阶段触觉注意力对接触丰富任务均至关重要。

Conclusion: VT-WAM通过显式建模触觉形变动力学并利用接触门控机制在关键时刻引导触觉注意力，有效提升了接触丰富操作任务的成功率，为视觉-触觉策略设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Contact-rich manipulation requires policies to react to local deformation, pressure, slip, and friction, yet these cues are temporally sparse and often invisible in visual observations. Existing visual-tactile policies usually feed tactile observations directly into action prediction, but rarely model tactile deformation dynamics during action generation. In this paper, we introduce VT-WAM, a Visual-Tactile World Action Model that jointly learns future visual prediction, tactile deformation prediction, and action prediction within a unified flow matching framework. In particular, VT-WAM introduces (1) Asymmetric Mixture-of-Transformers (MoT) attention to bridge a first-frame visual anchor with temporal tactile dynamics, and (2) contact-gated Action-Visual-Tactile Attention Guidance (AVTAG) to encourage action queries to rely on tactile evidence during contact phases. Across six real-world contact-rich manipulation tasks, VT-WAM achieves a 71.67% average success rate, outperforming Fast-WAM by 26.67% and OmniVTLA by 35.84%. Ablations demonstrate that modeling tactile deformation dynamics and guiding contact-phase tactile attention are both important for contact-rich tasks. Project website: https://vt-wam.github.io/.

</details>
